## <a name="windows-server-2003-r2"></a><span data-ttu-id="0822d-696">Windows Server 2003 R2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0822d-696">Windows Server 2003 R2</span></span>

-   [<span data-ttu-id="0822d-697">Attributs</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0822d-697">Attributes</span></span>](#windows-server-2003-r2-attributes)
